server.js:import express from 'express';
server.js:import { createServer as createViteServer } from 'vite';
server.js:import path from 'path';
server.js:
server.js:// Instantiate yahooFinance for v3
server.js:const yf = new yahooFinance();
server.js:
server.js:async function startServer() {
server.js:  const app = express();
server.js:  const PORT = 3000;
server.js:
server.js:  app.get('/api/market-data', async (req, res) => {
server.js:    try {
server.js:      const [qqq, spy, vix] = await Promise.all([
server.js:        yf.quote('QQQ'),
server.js:        yf.quote('SPY'),
server.js:        yf.quote('^VIX')
server.js:      ]);
server.js:
server.js:      res.json({
server.js:        qqq: {
server.js:          price: qqq.regularMarketPrice,
server.js:          change: qqq.regularMarketChangePercent,
server.js:          pe: qqq.trailingPE || 35.09,
server.js:        },
server.js:        spy: {
server.js:          price: spy.regularMarketPrice,
server.js:          change: spy.regularMarketChangePercent,
server.js:          pe: spy.trailingPE || 28.5,
server.js:        },
server.js:        vix: {
server.js:          price: vix.regularMarketPrice,
server.js:        }
server.js:      });
server.js:    } catch (error) {
server.js:      console.error('Error fetching market data:', error);
server.js:      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to fetch market data' });
server.js:    }
server.js:  });
server.js:
server.js:  if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
server.js:    const vite = await createViteServer({
server.js:      server: { middlewareMode: true },
server.js:      appType: 'spa',
server.js:    });
server.js:    app.use(vite.middlewares);
server.js:  } else {
server.js:    const distPath = path.join(process.cwd(), 'dist');
server.js:    app.use(express.static(distPath));
server.js:    app.get('*', (req, res) => {
server.js:      res.sendFile(path.join(distPath, 'index.html'));
server.js:    });
server.js:  }
